  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_f7cbc338-0b63-47a1-ba61-577c02b4ffb7'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

So she isn't prepared for this version of Reiner Kulti who shows up to her team's season: a quiet, reclusive shadow of the explosive, passionate man he'd once been.</span>

<div class='communityQuestion'>
<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/676147-questions-from-a-german-reader-i-liked">Questions from a German reader:
I liked the book very much (especially him calling her &quot;Schnecke&quot; all the time - so cute!) and I have a few questions. 
1. Was Michael Ballack the model for Kulti? 
2. Why did you place him with a club from Berlin (there is just one Bundesliga-Club in Berlin, and Hertha BSC is always at the verge of going down to second league)
3. Was Sal&#39;s name a reminiscence to Iker Casillas?</a>
</div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1267963057" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17846271246084267534"><b>Update: 5/4/19:</b><br/>You can find a really cute little epilogue scene here: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.marianazapata.com/kulti-outakes-from-the-future'>https://www.marianazapata.com/kulti-o...</a>... Thanks to Hulya for mentioning it in her review...just paying it forward for others to enjoy by doing the same.<br/><br/><b><u>Review:</u><br/><br/> Slooooooow Strong Stars</b><br/><br/>So not gonna lie, I went into this book completely blind. <br/><br/>I didn't read any other reviews on this before starting (which is typical for me). <br/><br/>Shit, I didn't even read the <i>blurb</i> (which is NOT typical for me). <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432574007i/14983359._SX540_.jpg' width='310' height='268.5' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>All I know is that I was "packing" my</span>
  <span id="freeText17846271246084267534" style="display:none"><b>Update: 5/4/19:</b><br>You can find a really cute little epilogue scene here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.marianazapata.com/kulti-outakes-from-the-future">https://www.marianazapata.com/kulti-o...</a>... Thanks to Hulya for mentioning it in her review...just paying it forward for others to enjoy by doing the same.<br><br><b><u>Review:</u><br><br> Slooooooow Strong Stars</b><br><br>So not gonna lie, I went into this book completely blind. <br><br>I didn't read any other reviews on this before starting (which is typical for me). <br><br>Shit, I didn't even read the <i>blurb</i> (which is NOT typical for me). <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432574007i/14983359._SX540_.jpg" width="310" height="268.5" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>All I know is that I was "packing" my kindle for my recent vacation and this book was kind of like that random extra bottle of full size conditioner you throw in your suitcase right before heading out the door, because you just <i>know</i> that little bullshit travel size is just NOT going to be enough. <br><br>All I knew when I one-clicked this is that I had read another book by this author - <i>Under Locke</i> - and I really enjoyed it. <br><br>So, like I said, I said fuck it and I went in blind.<br><br>And I'm glad I did, because otherwise I might have thrown this on the back burner, because Jesus F. Christ, this thing was LOOOOOOOONG. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432574007i/14983360._SX540_.jpg" width="659" height="399" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>But this was worth it.</b> <br><br>I REALLY enjoyed this book. <br><br>As a formerly serious athlete myself with a SUPER tight relationship with my own father, I related to Sal in spades. <br><br>Also, a benefit to the length of Zapata's stories (I went back and re-read parts of <i>Under Locke</i>, which I then remembered was also quite lengthy) is that you <i>really</i> get to know the characters after spending so much time with them and you <i>really</i> feel their connection.<br> <br>Another bonus? <br><br>The whole older male coach/younger female coachee dynamic. <br><br>I DIG it. <br><br>I am a SUCKER for it. <br><br>Me love it long time, every time. <br><br>My only complaint with this book is that it takes <i>forever</i> for anything to happen between these two outside of friendship. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432574616ra/14983420.gif" width="320" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For serious though. <br><br>I don't <i>always</i> need things to move fast or for their to be tons of steam, but I was starting to wonder if these two were <i>ever</i> going to get anywhere. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429900355i/14641767._SX540_.jpg" width="275.5" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Also, I REALLY wish this had had a more in-depth epilogue. <br><br>I felt a little cheated.<br><br>But anyways, long story not so short, if you are someone who typically likes things to move a little faster and needs a little more snap with your crackle, this might be a little too slow moving for you. <br><br>Otherwise, I say give this thing a go.<br><br>Just make sure you know it might take a year off your life to finish this. <br><br>Seriously.<br><br>I am a VERY fast reader and I think I noticed a gray hair on my head after finally finishing this thing. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1429796132ra/14631250.gif" width="500" height="374" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="17846271246084267534" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1429334938" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1429334938" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1429334938?book_show_action=true">Oct 30, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Christy by: </span>
      Jennifer Kyle
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11284813-christy?shelf=2016-audios">2016-audios</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1429334938" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1214300303103558526"><b>5+ German Chocolate Cake stars!</b> <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/430FE7A9-6BAA-4F49-95B4-360C263CED7C_zps0gysrv3r.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452731732i/17734354._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo 430FE7A9-6BAA-4F49-95B4-360C263CED7C_zps0gysrv3r.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“He was my coach. And I was his friend. Or something like that.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> OMG THIS BOOK! <i>Kulti</i> is one of those books that has been sitting on my TBR soon pile for months and months. I never found the time to read it, then I saw it was on audio so I made the time. I’ve read 14 books so far this year and it is by far the BEST book I’ve read so far. My first 5+ star read of the year! Kulti is a soccer book, but it’s so much more than that! It’s fun, heartwarmi</span>
  <span id="freeText1214300303103558526" style="display:none"><b>5+ German Chocolate Cake stars!</b> <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/430FE7A9-6BAA-4F49-95B4-360C263CED7C_zps0gysrv3r.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452731732i/17734354._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 430FE7A9-6BAA-4F49-95B4-360C263CED7C_zps0gysrv3r.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“He was my coach. And I was his friend. Or something like that.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> OMG THIS BOOK! <i>Kulti</i> is one of those books that has been sitting on my TBR soon pile for months and months. I never found the time to read it, then I saw it was on audio so I made the time. I’ve read 14 books so far this year and it is by far the BEST book I’ve read so far. My first 5+ star read of the year! Kulti is a soccer book, but it’s so much more than that! It’s fun, heartwarming and all around fantastic! <br><br>Kulti used to be Sal’s hero when she was a child. She was in love with this older soccer player and he gave her the drive to be the best she could be. Now she’s 27 and has been playing professionally for some time. Then she gets the news. That the elusive Reiner Kulti will be a coach for her team. Sal and Kulti have this fantastic love hate relationship to start with. I cannot tell you how many times this story made me laugh. Their back and forth banter was so well done. <br><i>
  <blockquote>"I'll be back.”<br><br>“Okay, Arnold.”<br><br>“He's Austrian, not German, you little shit.” </blockquote>
</i><br>The relationship between them is such a SLOW BUILD. It felt like it took an eternity to get to where they needed to be, but guess what? I didn’t even care. Not one bit. The friendship, the banter, the back and forth, the love that eventually developed… it was perfection. Sal and Kulti together- they were wonderful. He was an ass a lot of the book, but he was her ass. He could also be sweet though. When he calls her ‘my schnecke’ I melt… <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>”I had a man I respected that respected me, and he didn't care if the world knew we meant something to each other. Our friendship hadn't been given to either of us, we had worked at it. On top of that, I felt something for him even if he was egoistical, arrogant, stubborn pain in the ass. He was my egoistical, arrogant, stubborn pain in the ass.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Sal is one of the most fun, entertaining and refreshing heroines. She’s relatable, interesting, and being in her head is never annoying or boring. My man Kulti was not quite as lovable as Sal in the beginning, but by the end he had me swooning! And a special shout out to Sal’s dad. What a fantastic secondary character! It’s a long book, but I never felt like it was long, slow or boring. It was paced well. And written well. And all around AMAZING! Seriously, can you tell how much I loved this book?!?<br><br>This is for sure the best sports romance I’ve ever read. I can’t recommend it enough! And if you like audio, do yourself a favor and pick up the audible version. The narration was fantastic and Kulti’s German accent was done perfectly! <i>Kulti</i> gets 5+ stars from this reader!!! <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“You are my best friend, my love, my playmate and my teammate. You’ll have a team with me wherever we are, with whatever we’re playing.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/FE8306D8-CDC3-468F-91FE-F8BAA59AAA27_zpsgdzkwocq.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452731732i/17734355._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo FE8306D8-CDC3-468F-91FE-F8BAA59AAA27_zpsgdzkwocq.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="1214300303103558526" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1291106173" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1291106173" />
    <a title="Mo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11856352-mo"><img alt="Mo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1371247812p2/11856352.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1291106173?book_show_action=true">May 27, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mo" href="/user/show/11856352-mo">Mo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11856352-mo?shelf=favourite-ever">favourite-ever</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1291106173" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6700571294197204155">I loved this one, just loved it. First off, I love football ... that is "soccer" to a lot of you. I love the World Cup, the Champions League, The UEFA Championships... I was the girl who stood in the pissing rain at Terryland Park to watch Galway United because my then boyfriend, now husband, supported the team. The FA Cup Final is on this weekend and I will be glued to it, even though I don't support either team in the final...<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432935193i/15025975._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>He annoyed me, but I was also annoyed with myself for letting his</b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText6700571294197204155" style="display:none">I loved this one, just loved it. First off, I love football ... that is "soccer" to a lot of you. I love the World Cup, the Champions League, The UEFA Championships... I was the girl who stood in the pissing rain at Terryland Park to watch Galway United because my then boyfriend, now husband, supported the team. The FA Cup Final is on this weekend and I will be glued to it, even though I don't support either team in the final...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432935193i/15025975._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>He annoyed me, but I was also annoyed with myself for letting his attitude bother me.” </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I do love my smexy times in books but if you are looking for some hot loving and major sex scenes here you will be disappointed. I did not care. I loved the build up of their relationship, their banter. He had secrets. She had secrets... <br><br><blockquote> <b><i>When the man you worshipped as a kid becomes your coach, it’s supposed to be the greatest thing in the world. Keywords: supposed to. <br>It didn’t take a week for twenty-seven-year-old Sal Casillas to wonder what she’d seen in the international soccer icon—why she’d ever had his posters on her wall, or ever envisioned marrying him and having super-playing soccer babies. </i></b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432935193i/15025976.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>We had the trials and tribulations of training, the play offs to try and get to the finals. The rivalry with other teams. Do you have to be a football fan to enjoy this book? I don't think so ... then again, I was the Mom who was signing her 4 year olds up for the local football leagues. And they loved it. They still love football (soccer). They played for Varsity and Junior Varsity at school, got to travel to different countries with their school. I was the one who paid a fortune when our National team had a new jersey released.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432935193i/15025977._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I loved Sal and her family. Loved her Dad's passion for the game. I grew up with a Dad and two brother who were football fanatics. Highlight of the week used to be Saturday nights watching MOTD (Match of the Day).<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>This was like the best dream and the worst nightmare all wrapped into one beautiful package</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432935193i/15025978._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I really feel I could wax lyrical about this book. I really don't know what it was about it that I loved... as soon as I started it, I did not want to stop. Heads up, its a long book.... but I never lost interest in it.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"I care about things," he said.<br>"Oh? Like what?"<br>"Winning."</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432935193i/15025979.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Another little football story... USA 94. Yes, the USA did host the World Cup. Ireland qualified. My brother, who worked for American Airlines at the time won 2 airline ticket and 2 match tickets to Dallas to see Brazil versus the Netherlands. First class flights, five star hotel... flights from London to Dallas. Himself used to be a huge Netherlands fan when he was younger. He even had the jersey. My brother rang me to ask me if I wanted to go... I thought about it ... for 2 seconds ... then I asked him if Himself could go with him instead of me. Now is that not true love??? no wonder he is still married to me, after 23 years... I will hold that over his head, the fact that I gave up a ticket to Dallas so that he could go.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432935193i/15025980.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Ok, better shut up now. I will definitely be checking out more by this author. Whether you are football fan or not ... that's SOCCER to some of you ladies or gents ... I highly recommend this book. I think the title is a bit off-putting but that's just me.<br><br>Now, lets have one more last picture of KULTI (Xabi Alonso, the sexiest football player ever)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432935193i/15025981._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432840074i/15011225._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432935193i/15025982._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I will dedicate my review to Bill O'Heirlihy.... (Bill O'Herlihy (26 September 1938 – 25 May 2015) was an Irish television broadcaster and public relations executive. He was best known for his broadcasts for Raidió Teilifís Éireann (RTÉ), mainly covering sporting events.) His funeral was today. I grew up with his commentating on all our major football achievements ... and losses.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432936165i/15026114._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="6700571294197204155" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1508737635" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1508737635" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1508737635?book_show_action=true">Feb 01, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/29427515-kulti">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=rich-guys">rich-guys</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=forbidden-romance">forbidden-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=age-difference">age-difference</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=childhood-loves">childhood-loves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=hate-that-i-love-them">hate-that-i-love-them</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=might-piss-your-pants-laughing">might-piss-your-pants-laughing</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1508737635" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5119510514784214428">Check out more of my reviews at <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.bookaddicthaven.com'>www.bookaddicthaven.com</a><br/><br/>I've had this book sitting on my TBR for a long time. I had put off reading it for a few reasons, but the most notable reasons being that: 1) I am not a sports fan - at all- and I was worried I wouldn't enjoy it since this story was centered on two athletes; and 2) I was worried that I'd be disappointed after reading so many fantastic reviews for this book. Now that I've read it, I can say that neither of those concerns ended up coming to fr</span>
  <span id="freeText5119510514784214428" style="display:none">Check out more of my reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.bookaddicthaven.com">www.bookaddicthaven.com</a><br /><br />I've had this book sitting on my TBR for a long time. I had put off reading it for a few reasons, but the most notable reasons being that: 1) I am not a sports fan - at all- and I was worried I wouldn't enjoy it since this story was centered on two athletes; and 2) I was worried that I'd be disappointed after reading so many fantastic reviews for this book. Now that I've read it, I can say that neither of those concerns ended up coming to fruition.<br /><br />I listened to the Audible version of this book and I thought that it was fabulous. I loved the humor and the wittiness of the heroine, Sal Casillas. Kulti was a real piece of work at times and I loved that Sal wasn't afraid to call him out on his assholery. (Yep! I'm making that a word.) <br /><br />Sal and Kulti were a great pair. I spent a lot of time laughing my butt off at Sal's inner monologue. She was just so "human" that it was hard not to love her.<br /><br />On the other hand, Reiner Kulti was an acquired taste. He was the polar opposite of the easy-going Sal. He was wound tight, closed-off and outright rude for most of this book. However, little by little, a softer side of him was revealed.<br /><br />To say that this book was a slow-burn is putting it mildly. This story seemed to go on forever. I enjoyed it immensely, but I did think that it could have been trimmed down a little. <br /><br />The only other thing that I would've changed was the ending. Don't get me wrong, I liked the way everything played out. I just wanted more. It took so long for Sal and Kulti to get their HEA and after all the time spent describing every detail of every game, I felt like more time should've been dedicated to them as a couple. After all, I waited long enough to get there.<br /><br />Everything considered, I thought that this was a fantastic story. I was pleasantly surprised to find out that all of my worries had been completely misplaced. I enjoyed every minute of this book. If you've been putting it off like I did, don't.</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_3354290993" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3354290993" />
    <a title=" Teodora " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69603149-teodora"><img alt=" Teodora " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1582144281p2/69603149.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3354290993?book_show_action=true">Aug 01, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Teodora " class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Teodora " href="/user/show/69603149-teodora"> Teodora </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69603149-teodora?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69603149-teodora?shelf=on-app">on-app</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69603149-teodora?shelf=adult-new-adult">adult-new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69603149-teodora?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3354290993" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10148933484962770571">4.25/5 ⭐<br/><br/><b>Full review on my Blog:</b> <a href='https://thedacianshewolf.home.blog/2020/08/25/kulti-by-mariana-zapata/' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Dacian She-Wolf</a> 🐺<br/><br/>I – an occasional die-hard football fan who just discovered her passion for a good romantic comedy – to sleep on this? <br/>Sis, not on my watch.<br/><br/>About Zapata I’ve heard a couple of times and I was not convinced that I would ever pick up one of her books. But this one begged to differ. Because I picked it up and I actually enjoyed it.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1591185065ra/29587091.gif' width='327' height='241' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><br/>There is more of this book than its sports-related topic and the fact that it was supposed to be some romantic li</span>
  <span id="freeText10148933484962770571" style="display:none">4.25/5 ⭐<br><br><b>Full review on my Blog:</b> <a href="https://thedacianshewolf.home.blog/2020/08/25/kulti-by-mariana-zapata/" rel="nofollow noopener">The Dacian She-Wolf</a> 🐺<br><br>I – an occasional die-hard football fan who just discovered her passion for a good romantic comedy – to sleep on this? <br>Sis, not on my watch.<br><br>About Zapata I’ve heard a couple of times and I was not convinced that I would ever pick up one of her books. But this one begged to differ. Because I picked it up and I actually enjoyed it.<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1591185065ra/29587091.gif" width="327" height="241" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>There is more of this book than its sports-related topic and the fact that it was supposed to be some romantic little story happening there. There are some issues exposed that some might not know of or care about. But on some level, I do.<br><br>I am not the biggest fan of this apotheosis when it comes to football players. I mean, it really takes hard work and talent and a lot of sacrifices to get there, of course, but isn’t that the case with all of the other sports? Not a single sport out there is easy to perform on a grand scale so why kicking the ball around is worth more money? And especially, why is it like this only for men? <br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1591185065ra/29587092.gif" width="391" height="208" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>(Keep in mind that I don't attack anyone here, I am just trying to understand how things work and I seem to think that rhetorical questions help me)<br><br>Women play football too. And damn well, I might add. So why is it that women are trashed like that, not taken seriously as real athletes and paid "enough" to force them to take another job to pay their taxes?<br><br>Well, this is one of the issues in this book and the story behind a woman who plays professional football – Sal Casillas – and this book’s Fußballgott, Sal’s idol, Reiner Kulti.<br><br>Also, it isn’t only about how poorly treated Sal is here, but it is also about what fame has to bring to someone like Kulti. It is not pretty either.<br><br>It is interesting to follow though, if you ask me.<br><br>Sal and Kulti’s relationship is actually really credible. Everything is taken step by step, the friendship is clearly outlined first and then, by the end, everything falls neatly into place. A bit too conveniently, a small cynical part of me wants to say. But it feels like a nice dream (that we all have at one point – you know, that wild dream that you almost not dare think about but secretly, deeply wish for) that just comes true. And to hell with all, I am a sucker for nice dreams that come true! Good people deserve their wishes answered, even if they are spoken only inside their hearts!<br><br>Sure, Sal is just too amazing for her own good and Kulti is a total cocky asshole – a bit too possessive – but they actually fit together so well I just can’t help but cheer for them. Zapata really made a neat job with those two.<br><br>Sure, there were certain aspects that bothered me a bit, one of them being that it took me too much to actually get into the storyline and another being the fact that sometimes everything happening felt a tiny bit too surreal.<br><br>But you know what made up for everything? Sal’s relationship with her dad. I mean, her dad is such a mood and he is amazing and I loved seeing a strong father-daughter relationship in a book. It is worth millions, I am telling you.<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1591185065ra/29587093.gif" width="369" height="222" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>For my seventh contemporary romance novel in a month, this was mildly rom, mildly com, and thoroughly enjoyable. I am glad I picked it up!<br><br>(<a href="https://urcdn.eu/styles/b5481dd5-af38-4c10-9a83-73a6737e6e7a_original?b" rel="nofollow noopener">Book-styled</a>)</span>
  <a data-text-id="10148933484962770571" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1292810599" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1292810599" />
    <a title="Mysza" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14262653-mysza"><img alt="Mysza" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1433922560p2/14262653.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1292810599?book_show_action=true">May 29, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mysza" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mysza" href="/user/show/14262653-mysza">Mysza</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14262653-mysza?shelf=favorite-read">favorite-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1292810599" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10060518318139459253"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Every single thing that has ever happened in my life has led me here, Sal. Destiny is a ladder, a series of steps that takes you where you're supposed to go. I am the man that I am, and I have done the things that I've done, to get me to you."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433801756i/15144765._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>The story is about twenty-seven-year-old Sal Casillas, who is a professional football (or soccer for some of you) player. Throughout her child and teenage years, she had a big crush on now retired German player - Reiner Kulti, he was the reaso</span>
  <span id="freeText10060518318139459253" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Every single thing that has ever happened in my life has led me here, Sal. Destiny is a ladder, a series of steps that takes you where you're supposed to go. I am the man that I am, and I have done the things that I've done, to get me to you."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433801756i/15144765._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The story is about twenty-seven-year-old Sal Casillas, who is a professional football (or soccer for some of you) player. Throughout her child and teenage years, she had a big crush on now retired German player - Reiner Kulti, he was the reason she started training football in the first place. Years went by and while growing up, she grew out of this infatuation. Now, she is playing for Houston Pipers and guess who took a position as a new assistant coach in her team? Kulti is a dick from the moment he starts working with the Pipers, but our Sal here won't take his shit calmly and quickly calls him on it. That's how their journey starts.<br><br>And be aware, the book is long and their journey is long but oh so worth it. And though long it is, I devoured it. The writing is excellent, flows naturally, you turn page by page and never get bored. It's a classic example of slow build up, but it is exactly what made this book magical for me. The tension, the anticipation, it worked so fine here. Sal and Kulti started as kind of enemies, went to friends and then naturally, when they were ready, became lovers.<br><br>I loved their banter and bickering. Kulti was very serious and grumpy most of the time but he also had a healthy dose of humor in him, and Sal was no worse.<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I'll be back.<br>Okay, Arnold.<br>He's Austrian, not German, you little shit."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Trust me; I've had the urge to punch you in the face a time or five."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Have I told you that you remind me of a splinter I can't remove? You're incredibly annoying."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I was in love with this pumpernickel. God help me, I think I wanted to cry."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>Sal was such a likeable heroine, she was sweet, sincere, helpful and generally a nice girl. She, as no one else, was able to get close to Kulti, gained his trust and made him open up more. <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I had a man I respected that respected me, and he didn't care if the world knew we meant something to each other. Our friendship hadn't been given to either of us, we had worked at it. On top of that, I felt something for him even if he was egoistical, arrogant, stubborn pain in the ass. He was my egoistical, arrogant, stubborn pain in the ass."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>Kulti, well, he was a man of a few words, and I totally dig that brooding, grumpy kind of heroes. He never said much but once he opened his mouth, here's what came out. Don't you just get swooned on the spot?<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"My schnecke. My little snail, do you know that's what it means? It's a term of affection in my country. My love. My snail. I don't want to waste more time. I have nothing to hide and neither do you."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I've been waiting, and I will keep on waiting until the time is right. You are my equal, my partner, my teammate, my best friend. I've done so many stupid things that you've made me regret - things I hope you will forgive me for and look beyond - but this, waiting a little longer for the love of my life, I can do.<br>You are the most honest, warm, loving person I know. Your loyalty and friendship amazes me every day. I have never wanted anything more in my life than I want your love, and I don't want to share that with anyone. I haven't done a single thing in my life to deserve you, schnecke, but I will never give up on you, and I won't let you give up on me."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>And I loved the names she called him. I have Germany right across the border, been a few times, know the language a bit and I think her nicknames were so darn cute. Just a few...<i>the human Berlin Wall, sauerkraut, German bratwurst, Chocolate Cake, Goddamn frankfurter, German tank, pumpernickel, pretzel face...</i> Kulti didn't stay indebted for long and came up with <i>Taco</i> for her.<br><br>And if you read for the nookie than you might be disappointed, because there is almost none, almost... but those two scenes that were here, were effin hot! And the whole anticipation thing was so wonderful that it easily made up for lack of too much sex. And you know what? I didn't care, cause when the book is as good as this one you will get by without it.<br><br>Well, to sum up, I would give it perfect ten stars if I could. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1433801756ra/15144766.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>And in the end, I just want to say this is why I love GR and my friends here, because I would have probably not read this book if not for Mo and Didi. I've had my sight on it for a long time but never got to it. If I didn't see their updates and reviews, I would probably never read it. So big shout out to you girls, thanks for updates:)<br><br><b>Guest reviewer at</b><br><a href="http://readmore-sleepless.blogspot.gr/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431941645i/14885109._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a> </span>
  <a data-text-id="10060518318139459253" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer8310281157838664083"><b>4 Stars</b><br/><br/>Boy this was....<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1482261581ra/21499130.gif' width='500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Long. Really, really looooong. And slooooooow. <br/><br/>I'm not going to lie. I was struggling in the beginning until I reached the 30% mark and then finally, <i>finally</i> the story caught my interested. <br/><br/>And I liked it. I liked it A LOT. Because, let me quote from the book: "What a fucking douche-bag!"<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1482264875ra/21499546.gif' width='500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>He's perfect.<br/><br/>It's amazing how realistically the author portrays the slow development of their love and relationship. It’s also amazing how she managed to use almost every possible elemen</span>
  <span id="freeText8310281157838664083" style="display:none"><b>4 Stars</b><br><br>Boy this was....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1482261581ra/21499130.gif" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Long. Really, really looooong. And slooooooow. <br><br>I'm not going to lie. I was struggling in the beginning until I reached the 30% mark and then finally, <i>finally</i> the story caught my interested. <br><br>And I liked it. I liked it A LOT. Because, let me quote from the book: "What a fucking douche-bag!"<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1482264875ra/21499546.gif" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>He's perfect.<br><br>It's amazing how realistically the author portrays the slow development of their love and relationship. It’s also amazing how she managed to use almost every possible element so popular in the contemporary romance genre today and create a perfect <i>enemies-turn-friends-turn-lovers coach-player forbidden loved-you-from-afar-since-childhood age-gap sports </i>romance featuring a strong heroine and a silent, broody, jerk hero without being over the top or too cliché. <br><br>If you’re a fan of slow burn character-driven romances I highly recommend this book.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1482265436ra/21499616.gif" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>QUICK REVIEW:</b><br><br><b>Enjoyment:</b>: 4/5<br><b>Writing style:</b> 4/5<br><b>Storyline:</b> 4/5<br><b>Hero:</b> 4.5/5 <br><b>Heroine:</b> 3.5/5<br><b>Secondary characters:</b> 4/5 <br><b>Hotness/chemistry:</b> 4/5 <br><b>Romance:</b> 5/5 <br><b>Angst:</b> 3/5<br><b>Darkness level:</b> 1/5<br><b>Humor:</b> 3/5<br><b> Depth of the book:</b> 5/5<br><b>POV:</b> heroine, 1st person<br><b> Triggers:</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[None <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510504825i/24426022._SX540_.jpg" width='400"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1238827071" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1238827071" />
    <a title="Didi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6082482-didi"><img alt="Didi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459297426p2/6082482.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1238827071?book_show_action=true">Mar 27, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Didi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Didi" href="/user/show/6082482-didi">Didi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">EVERYONE!!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=best-of-2015">best-of-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=betrayal">betrayal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=what-a-jock">what-a-jock</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=unable-to-put-down">unable-to-put-down</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1238827071" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4844450548192194141">10+++++ STARS!!!!!<br/><br/>I haven't read a book in awhile that has left me so affected, so happy, so...GAH! I LOVED IT, LOVED IT, LOVED IT. I'm feeling particularly confused right now because I want to say so much but I don't know how! So to save time and space, I'll point out what I loved, adored, gobbled up so much:<br/><br/>1. SOCCER, SOCCER, SOCCER. Love that sport. The World Cup? It's a Holiday at my house where everything can wait until 'The Game' is over. Many books are soccer related, right? Sure, but not</span>
  <span id="freeText4844450548192194141" style="display:none">10+++++ STARS!!!!!<br /><br />I haven't read a book in awhile that has left me so affected, so happy, so...GAH! I LOVED IT, LOVED IT, LOVED IT. I'm feeling particularly confused right now because I want to say so much but I don't know how! So to save time and space, I'll point out what I loved, adored, gobbled up so much:<br /><br />1. SOCCER, SOCCER, SOCCER. Love that sport. The World Cup? It's a Holiday at my house where everything can wait until 'The Game' is over. Many books are soccer related, right? Sure, but not like this. This felt like I was in the game, it was realistic and amazingly, details of the sport were sporadically blended in and never took over the incredible, romantic storyline. <br /><br />2. The older man/younger woman. Sure, it's also quite common, but a girl who's looked up to and admired a renowned and iconic soccer superstar, then to have said star become her best friend and slowly so much, much more? FANTASTICAL. I loved it. I can't even...<br /><br />3. The slow, molasses worthy, pack a lunch, SLOW build up. I'll be honest, if you want the bang, bang, thank you ma'am, you ain't gonna get it here. This was a great example of using patience as a virtue. But damn, does it deliver in spades when they get together. The beauty is, the sexual tension and nuances of Kulti's and Sal's fantastic relationship was enough, it was beautiful, amazing, phenomenal and had my heart melting over and over...and that was when they were friends! When they got together? The steam, although not long was TO DIE FOR. The epilogue had me in tears, blissed out tears.<br /><br />4. The writing...exquisite. I could not put this down, and this baby was long! But incredibly, when I finished I wanted to cry because I wanted more!<br /><br />5. Sal. I like, not love most of the heroines I read about, but this awesome, kick-ass chick was amazing. I loved Sal as much as I loved Kulti and he was THE MAN. Sal was everything I've ever striven to be. She was the best person I wish I knew. And Kutli? Rough around the edges, yes, but a diamond underneath...sigh.<br /><br />If I'm building this up then sorry if you'll be disappointed. But sometimes a book just jives with you and affects you in a way that's difficult to put in words. I dreamt about this book when I wasn't reading it, okay? I squeezed in time just to read a damn page! It never dragged, never wallowed and never let me down. I can't say enough. Just remember the love between these two is slow to deliver though you see it in all they do, all the time. The relationship Sal had with her dad was exemplary, touching and pulled at my heartstrings. If I could eat this book I would, I know I sound crazy. But seriously, the BEST I've read all year, possibly in the last two years. YES, THAT GOOD. <br /><br />I'm checking out everything this author has written, up to and including any pamphlets she may have penned in her early writing career. This was funny, laugh out loud hilarious! Quoting what Sal called Kulti would look weird out of context ( eg. A German Bratwurst ), but I had to stop and catch my breath a few times! It was engaging, that word created alone for how this book kept me hooked, and incredibly romantic. I can't say enough but I'll stop here because I'm gonna start repeating myself, so yeah...FREAKING LOVED IT to the moon and back!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="4844450548192194141" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1312812298" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1312812298" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1312812298?book_show_action=true">Jun 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1312812298" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3536993289192852837"><b> 4.5 Stars </b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>”He was my coach. And I was his friend. Or something like that.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>Truth be told, I’m not a huge soccer fan but I played sports in my early years so reading about a professional female player is a total win for me. This sports theme book is centered around a full soccer season taking our heroine and her new coach through a slow building friendship to more. <br/><br/>Sal, our heroine is a professional soccer player who finds out that her team’s new assistant coach will be none othe</span>
  <span id="freeText3536993289192852837" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 Stars </b><br><br><b>
  <i>”He was my coach. And I was his friend. Or something like that.”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>Truth be told, I’m not a huge soccer fan but I played sports in my early years so reading about a professional female player is a total win for me. This sports theme book is centered around a full soccer season taking our heroine and her new coach through a slow building friendship to more. <br><br>Sal, our heroine is a professional soccer player who finds out that her team’s new assistant coach will be none other than Reiner Kulti. Kulti is a world famous retired German soccer star who Sal had been obsessed with as a young girl. Reiner Kulti was well written in his broody, rude clipped tone. I loved their interactions and rejoiced in the friendship and dreamed of their friendship heading into more.<br><br><b>
  <i>”That was my first time using a lawn mower.'<br>I fucking knew it!! I didn't say that of course, instead I stuck with a very grown up, 'Oh really?”</i>
</b><br><br>Reiner was slow to reveal himself but his appreciation for Sal’s talent and the woman she is was worth the wait as the two come to the end of the season with strong feelings for one another.<br> <br><b>
  <i>”Hug me back,” the accented voice demanded from above.”</i>
</b><br><br>Overall, the writing, delivery and the humor were all very well done. The banter, those nicknames and Sal’s dad were also so very enjoyable. At times yes I have to admit the story was slow going for me but I held out hope that there was more behind this hot German superstar. In the end, he more than delivered in the love department and in the bedroom!<br> <br><b>
  <i>"You are my best friend, my love, my playmate and my teammate. You'll have a team with me wherever we are, with whatever we're playing." </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491750334ra/22442662.gif" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="3536993289192852837" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1509150104" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12686407835628822297"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459012530i/18560866._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Oh. My.</i> <b>So many lessons learnt reading <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24044596.Kulti' title='Kulti by Mariana Zapata' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kulti</a></b>. <br/><br/>➊ <b>Sociopaths have a soft spot for blinking</b>. A lot. 34 times for Kulti to be exact, and 86 times total. Now that's a bit much, don't you think? <br/><br/>➋ For the first time <i>ever</i>, my eyes twitched at the recurrent use of the same words to name a character. <b>Someone save me from <i>The German</i></b>. Like please. This is getting old.<br/><br/>➌ <b>There are such things as too-much vague adjectives to describe eyes</b>. <i>"Light-colored"</i>, <i>"warm-colored"</i> (whatever THAT means), just make a poi</span>
  <span id="freeText12686407835628822297" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459012530i/18560866._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Oh. My.</i> <b>So many lessons learnt reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24044596.Kulti" title="Kulti by Mariana Zapata" rel="nofollow noopener">Kulti</a></b>. <br><br>➊ <b>Sociopaths have a soft spot for blinking</b>. A lot. 34 times for Kulti to be exact, and 86 times total. Now that's a bit much, don't you think? <br><br>➋ For the first time <i>ever</i>, my eyes twitched at the recurrent use of the same words to name a character. <b>Someone save me from <i>The German</i></b>. Like please. This is getting old.<br><br>➌ <b>There are such things as too-much vague adjectives to describe eyes</b>. <i>"Light-colored"</i>, <i>"warm-colored"</i> (whatever THAT means), just make a point already. <br><br>➍ No, Sal, you <b>can't</b> <i>"[miss] the glance he took at [your] mouth. [Miss] the way he fisted his hand as he pried it off [your] shoulder"</i>. Because <i>Hello</i>, first POV narrative. <b>You don't get to choose when you are omniscient</b>. <br><br>➎ You can be attracted to a cardboard male-lead and yet be interesting on your own. <b>Sal sure earns both of my two stars</b> : she's strong, fierce, loyal to her family, and actually has girl friends. <br><br>➏ But <b>I never liked Sal more than when she called The King Kulti on his shit</b>. That girl has a spine. Kudos to her, really. I might have been cheering loudly at some parts (the bratwurst did it *smiles slowly*) She even managed to make me laugh with her banter (Kulti doesn't count, because really, the guy barely ever opens his mouth)<br><br>➐ As for the slut-shaming, I'll give <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5760202.Mariana_Zapata" title="Mariana Zapata" rel="nofollow noopener">Mariana Zapata</a> the <b>benefit of the doubt</b>, because Sal did reprimand herself every time she let herself go all insulting in her head. I'm watching you, though.<br><br>➑ <i>Big. Girl. Socks.</i> GAH. It was funny the first time, not too much the 17th. <br><br>➒ If <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24044596.Kulti" title="Kulti by Mariana Zapata" rel="nofollow noopener">Kulti</a> was meant to make me interested in football players, what a fail it is. I have yet to meet a male-lead who compete with <i>The German</i> fucking <b><u>blandness</u>.</b> <b>Part asshole, part wild animal, part pot plant or something, Kulti sure didn't restore football players' image as far as I'm concerned</b>. Trust me, I'm French. I know way too-much football players for my own good. Yep. I'm a generalizing jerk. Sue me. (nah, alright, some are pretty nice, and looking at <i>The German</i>, I feel a little pissed on their behalf)<br><br>➓ <b>Read it if you don't mind terrible writing, snail like pacing, almost no chemistry, and loads and loads of sport talk</b>. I, for one, didn't care for the first, have yet to find the point of this, and enjoy football as the next person - hahaha who am I kidding? Have you freaking <i>seen</i> France's team? The guys went on strike for crying out loud *roll-eyes*. Actually, do you want to know a secret? I've been rooting for Germany for ten years. <br><br><i>Gah</i>. Trust me, <b>the irony is not lost on me</b>.<br><br>*facepalm* <br><br><i>"Tell me. Do you want my fingers in your warm pussy?"</i><br><br>Definitely not. <br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i><br><blockquote>
  <a href="https://meetthebookworld.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487851828i/22057164._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote></span>

<div id="review_1976761423" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1976761423" />
    <a title="Cristina Monica" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14596170-cristina-monica"><img alt="Cristina Monica" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589617514p2/14596170.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1976761423?book_show_action=true">Apr 19, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cristina Monica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cristina Monica" href="/user/show/14596170-cristina-monica">Cristina Monica</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1976761423" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14473936915041566790">What an adventure. Almost six hundred pages long. I feel like I know Sal inside and out. God, I haven’t read a book this voluminous in a long time, because I lack patience. But surprisingly, I didn’t mind taking my time with this one. <br/><br/>Every chapter was a new surprise. I enjoyed the genuine writing style. It was not at all pretentious. I wouldn’t say it was incredibly lyrical either. In fact, it was pretty repetitive when you think about it, but it was so accessible I was always in the mood for i</span>
  <span id="freeText14473936915041566790" style="display:none">What an adventure. Almost six hundred pages long. I feel like I know Sal inside and out. God, I haven’t read a book this voluminous in a long time, because I lack patience. But surprisingly, I didn’t mind taking my time with this one. <br /><br />Every chapter was a new surprise. I enjoyed the genuine writing style. It was not at all pretentious. I wouldn’t say it was incredibly lyrical either. In fact, it was pretty repetitive when you think about it, but it was so accessible I was always in the mood for it.<br /><br />Sports romance. How can you not like that? Actually, I picked this book up because I heard it was a slow romance and that’s exactly what I needed. I took a long break from new adult books because most of them have insta-love or insta-lust and I just couldn’t take it anymore. I needed out. But now I want in again, because Zapata has reawakened my interest in new adult books.<br /><br />How refreshing that the main character is a football player herself. I’m just tired of silly, or even intelligent, girls falling for jocks. I mean, it’s a fantasy, I do get it, and I guess those guys are indeed quite sexy, but it’s become sort of a cliché for me. That’s why I loved this so much. Sal plays football professionally. So does her love interest.<br /><br />But get this: they don’t kiss in the first chapter. Or fifth. Or tenth. Or twentieth. You get the idea. This is a true slow romance. Don’t worry about it, though. I know many people are bored without romance in their reads. This isn’t like that. Sal and Kulti—hence the title, grrr—are enemies, then friends, then best friends, then lovers. Isn’t that wonderful? It makes the love story even more realistic.<br /><br />It’s true that everything is slow, but so is life. What’s fortunate about that is the fact that because everything is so realistically-paced, there is obvious progression in the story and great characterization. We actually get to know the heroine very well. I could definitely see this becoming a successful and addictive TV series. Oh I just love love-hate relationships. Gimme, gimme. <br /><br />Unlike sixteen-year-old Sal, I’m not crazy about Kulti. I mean, he is sexy, but he’s not really of the romantic type. Sure, he’s serious, giving him a mysterious vibe, and I was curious about him, and yeah he and Sal did have a relationship they both enjoyed. But I could never date a guy who would call me names—idiot, stupid—even if in a playful, affectionate manner. And I prefer someone who smiles frequently. Bah, he’s not my type. That’s why I can’t give this book 5 full stars. And also because the writing style could have been better. But it was amazing still. Read it, buddies. <br /><br /><a href="https://hitormissbooks.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/c/LolaReviewer" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a>Twitter</a> | <a>Instagram</a> | <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/105021852309973899120/posts" rel="nofollow noopener">Google+</a> | <a href="https://www.bloglovin.com/blogs/hit-miss-books-12564715" rel="nofollow noopener">Bloglovin’</a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14473936915041566790" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2290892790" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2290892790" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2290892790?book_show_action=true">Feb 10, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=2contemporary-lovestories">2contemporary-lovestories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=sports">sports</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2290892790" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17731594925983538004">This book goes straight to the shelf with my favorite books because it combines three of the things that I value most in life:<br/><b>
  <u>1.	FOOTBALL<br/>2.	TRUE LOVE and<br/>3.	FATE</u>
</b><br/><br/>First of all, I love football. Or soccer, as it is called on the other side of the Atlantic Ocean. I think that it is the bestest sport that has been created on the face of Earth.<br/>And you may think that I will tell you now a heartbreaking story about my childhood, how I used to go to the stadium and watch my favorite team kick ass ever</span>
  <span id="freeText17731594925983538004" style="display:none">This book goes straight to the shelf with my favorite books because it combines three of the things that I value most in life:<br /><b>
  <u>1.	FOOTBALL<br />2.	TRUE LOVE and<br />3.	FATE</u>
</b><br /><br />First of all, I love football. Or soccer, as it is called on the other side of the Atlantic Ocean. I think that it is the bestest sport that has been created on the face of Earth.<br />And you may think that I will tell you now a heartbreaking story about my childhood, how I used to go to the stadium and watch my favorite team kick ass every Sunday. The truth is that I went to watch my first football game when I was much much older. And it was unbelievable great! You see, my father believed that girls are not supposed to go and watch football matches. So, thank God for television… <br /><br />On the other hand, although I was thirsty to watch my favorite team or the national team doing great in Europe, I had one disappointment after the other. Obviously Greece could not play good football internationally. I should have loved basketball more… Oh, well… <br />And not let me start about women’s football. <br /><br />UEFA Euro 2004. Greece is the European Champion against all odds. Thank you, thank you, thank you Otto Rehhagel. Otto was the best coach my national team ever had. <br />So you may understand now why <b>
  <u>I adore and respect German football coaches</u>
</b> – even Reiner Kulti, in our case, who (let’s face it) he may have been an excellent footballer…<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>He ran, and ran, and ran and by some miracle avoided every opposing player that went after him. He scored the most beautiful, ruthless goal in the top right corner of the net. The ball seemed to sail through the air with a one-way ticket to the record books.<br />My dad screamed. Eric yelled. The freaking stadium and the announcers lost it. This guy who had never played on such a platform had done what no one expected of him.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br />…but he was not a good enough coach. I am sure Sal Casillas, the best footballer in Pipers, can tell you all about it.<br /><br />Sal and Kulti (aka Taco and German Chocolate Cake) will firstly be trainee and trainer, then friend and best friend and then the miracle will happen.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“This is what matters. You are my gift, my second chance, and I will cherish you and your dream. I will protect both of you. <br />I’ve been waiting, and I will keep on waiting until the time is right. You are my equal, my partner, my teammate, my best friend. I’ve done so many stupid things that you’ve made me regret—things I hope you will forgive me for and look beyond— but this, waiting a little longer for the love of my life, I can do.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br />Between angst, family moments, hard training, commitment and passion, bad choices, careers that are ready to fly or to be destroyed; Kulti will manage to squeeze his life into Sal’s life. Not that Sal was not ready to love him. She was in love with him since before she knew what love it.<br /><br />But of course whatever was meant to be, it will always find a way.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Every single thing that has ever happened in my life has led me here, Sal. Destiny is a ladder, a series of steps that takes you where you’re supposed to go. I am the man that I am, and I have done the things that I’ve done, to get me to you.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br />I don’t think I want to say much about the story. I only want to emphasize that it is a sloooow-burn romance as most of Mariana Zapata’s books. <br />I never thought I would find a guy that talks less that Aiden Graves (The Wall of Winnipeg and Me) actually.<br /><br />Anyway, enjoy the book!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="17731594925983538004" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
