<div id="review_1152478634" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1152478634" />
    <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy"><img alt="Stacey is Sassy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474185067p2/12062194.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1152478634?book_show_action=true">Jan 02, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacey is Sassy" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy">Stacey is Sassy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/29427515-kulti">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=slow-burn">slow-burn</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=cranky-hero">cranky-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=cont-sports">cont-sports</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1152478634" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer667466592285960240"><b>Now I get it...</b><br/><br/>I knew about <i>Kulti</i>. I had read <i>Under Locke</i> by <i>Mariana Zapata</i> and really, really enjoyed it. When I heard that she had a new book coming out I was really excited. Then the whispers started. It’s a sllloooowwww burn romance and it’s about a female soccer player. Screeching to a halt…Say what??? Then, I started asking questions…so, how slow are we talking? Answer: Really, really slow. A female in sports…more determined, hard-working and extremely motivated. Hmmm, not really convinced</span>
  <span id="freeText667466592285960240" style="display:none"><b>Now I get it...</b><br><br>I knew about <i>Kulti</i>. I had read <i>Under Locke</i> by <i>Mariana Zapata</i> and really, really enjoyed it. When I heard that she had a new book coming out I was really excited. Then the whispers started. It’s a sllloooowwww burn romance and it’s about a female soccer player. Screeching to a halt…Say what??? Then, I started asking questions…so, how slow are we talking? Answer: Really, really slow. A female in sports…more determined, hard-working and extremely motivated. Hmmm, not really convinced to jump right in, think I’m going to hold off for a bit. So, I did. One thing leads to another and poor old Kulti got pushed back again and again. Then, I had an idea…why don’t I get the audio and listen to it instead?<br><br>Normally, when I listen to an audiobook, I’ve previously read the story but in this case, I was listening to it first. It was a very different experience. I had to really pay attention and I couldn’t stand leaving it for more than 24 hours. As <i>Kulti</i> is a fairly long story, I thought it would take me a lot longer to listen than it did. I was sucked in and desperate to see how things would play out. <br><br>The narrator has an easy voice to listen to. I did at times think she sounded a bit too young, but that could have more to do with her having an American accent. I find American women, in general, have very young and sweet voices. Anyways, the narrator did a fabulous job talking with different accents and I had no problems identifying when a character changed. If I was to find fault with the narration, the only difficulty I had was when the main character switched between dialogue and inner monologue. Besides that, it was all good.<br><br>I loved Sal. Her determination and focus were easy to believe and the highs and lows of dealing with her former young girl crush becoming her current coach were interesting. Sal just wants to play soccer. She must learn to treat him as normal, not as her first love and the man she dreamed of marrying. She also has to get past the fact that Kulti broke her brother’s leg years ago when they were playing soccer on opposing teams. Poor Sal has a lot to deal with. She is almost tongue-tied and the only way she can stop herself from being a blathering fool is to remind herself over and over again that Kulti poos and wees. Sal has to mind herself of that quite a bit.<br><br>Kulti comes into the <i>Houston Piper’s</i> world as the assistant coach. He doesn’t want to be there and makes it bloody obvious. He does nothing but stands on the sidelines and watch. It takes one of his players approaching him and telling him to pull his head out of his arse, before he starts doing his job. Kulti has a few issues he is dealing with behind the scene and unfortunately, Sal becomes the person to help him get on track. It cracked me up the way he just barges into her life and plants himself with no plans to leave at all. The sexual tension was obvious to me and I was just waiting (and waiting and waiting…) for things to start coming together.<br><br>Oh, the coming together made it so worthwhile. For such a cranky arse, Kulti sure does know how to make a lady swoon. He says all the right words and backs it all up with his actions. He is protective, caring and possessive with a desire to make things easy for Sal. Unfortunately, all of Sal’s problems stem from being friends with Kulti, so it’s not easy for him.<br><br>Yes, I probably shouldn’t have waited so long to read <i>Kulti</i> but it was a different experience listening instead of reading and I thoroughly enjoyed it. To top it all off, I was able to test the waters to see how I would go listening to an audiobook when I hadn’t read it first. Win, win all round.<br><br>I will definitely be reading more books by <i>Mariana Zapata</i> in the future.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1548709401i/26982519.jpg" width="300" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="667466592285960240" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1474697154?book_show_action=true">Dec 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish">UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

    <span class="greyText">Recommended to UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/34029210-suzie">Suzie</a>
  </div>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=2016-reads">2016-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=gift-from-friend">gift-from-friend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=own-have-read">own-have-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=format-audio-via-audible">format-audio-via-audible</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=author-mariana-zapata">author-mariana-zapata</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=format-kindle-or-kindle-compatible">format-kindle-or-kindle-compatible</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=must-read-author">must-read-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=sports-soccer">sports-soccer</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1474697154" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1085700344689250587"><br/>Full review now posted...<br/><br/><i>“Every single thing that has ever happened in my life has led me here, Sal. Destiny is a ladder, a series of steps that takes you where you’re supposed to go. I am the man that I am, and I have done the things that I’ve done, to get me to you.”</i><br/><br/><i>Kulti</i> is one of those difficult-to-review books, not because there’s anything wrong with it but because there is just so much “right” with it. There are so many things to gush about, so many things I want to share with you, but I w</span>
  <span id="freeText1085700344689250587" style="display:none"><br />Full review now posted...<br /><br /><i>“Every single thing that has ever happened in my life has led me here, Sal. Destiny is a ladder, a series of steps that takes you where you’re supposed to go. I am the man that I am, and I have done the things that I’ve done, to get me to you.”</i><br /><br /><i>Kulti</i> is one of those difficult-to-review books, not because there’s anything wrong with it but because there is just so much “right” with it. There are so many things to gush about, so many things I want to share with you, but I won’t deprive you of the enjoyment that’ll come as the story slowly unfolds revealing painful secrets from the past, and the peace that can come when you share those secrets with the people who care about you most.<br /><br />I’ve seen some reviewers say that this isn’t a romance novel, and I might agree with them, but only to a degree. The relationship - both emotional and sexual - between Reiner Kulti and Salomé Casillas is slow to grow, but it happens in such a mature, believable way that it’s one of the things I love most about the story. But make no mistake about it, there’s most definitely a romance here, and it’s beautiful - and hot!<br /><br />I’ll wrap it by saying that if you’re like me and not a big fan of the New Adult genre because of all the drama inherent in its stories, give this one a try. There's drama, yes, but it's not contrived and fits perfectly with this sports themed romance. <br /><br /><i>Kulti</i> is a stand-alone novel and so well done that you can bet I’ll be looking for more by Mariana Zapata!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1085700344689250587" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1736036239" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1736036239" />
    <a title="Tessa Bailey" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16757792-tessa-bailey"><img alt="Tessa Bailey" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442877672p2/16757792.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1736036239?book_show_action=true">Aug 22, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tessa Bailey" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tessa Bailey" href="/user/show/16757792-tessa-bailey">Tessa Bailey</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1736036239" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11451244915528979272">New favorite author. Hands down. I'm sure I can't say anything original here, because everyone loves this book, but I have to TRY. Because this book made me feel so many things. It was stellar. <br/><br/>One. Zapata's ability to really, honestly make me believe the heroine has no idea the hero would literally perish at her feet for a single touch...it's mind-blowing. And very difficult to pull off, especially when her heroines are so damn smart and emotionally mature. It makes the moment where they admit </span>
  <span id="freeText11451244915528979272" style="display:none">New favorite author. Hands down. I'm sure I can't say anything original here, because everyone loves this book, but I have to TRY. Because this book made me feel so many things. It was stellar. <br /><br />One. Zapata's ability to really, honestly make me believe the heroine has no idea the hero would literally perish at her feet for a single touch...it's mind-blowing. And very difficult to pull off, especially when her heroines are so damn smart and emotionally mature. It makes the moment where they admit their feelings CRAZY amazing. Like, fireworks during a grand slam amazing. <br /><br />Two. In both this book and The Wall of Winnipeg and Me, the hero and heroine make each other better people. Authentically, beautifully better. It happens over an extended period of time and each rung in the ladder to being their better selves is SO SATISFYING. Because they SHARE it. And it's balanced between the two characters. <br /><br />Three. I love heroines. I especially love them when they're loyal as hell. When I can depend on the heroine to act out of loyalty (whether to herself, a friend, family member or the hero) no matter what happens, I'm that author's fan for life. <br /><br />Go click this book STAT. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11451244915528979272" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1293361843" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1293361843" />
    <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27276528-liz"><img alt="✰ Liz ✰ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451097545p2/27276528.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1293361843?book_show_action=true">Dec 07, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Liz ✰ " href="/user/show/27276528-liz">✰ Liz ✰ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=athletic-god">athletic-god</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=forbidden-love">forbidden-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=girl-power">girl-power</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=best-couples">best-couples</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=best-leading-lady">best-leading-lady</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=alpha-male-love">alpha-male-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=love-this-author">love-this-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=2018-favorite">2018-favorite</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=beautiful-cover">beautiful-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1293361843" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12292476490552003384"><blockquote>
  <b>"I have so much to teach you, Taco."</b>
</blockquote><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1546366652i/26845944._SX540_.jpg' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Kulti</b> is another masterfully crafted slow burn contemporary romance from the slow burn queen Mariana Zapata. Sal Casillas is a professional soccer player living in Houston, Texas. She has always been driven to achieve great things. When the new season is beginning, imagine her horror and surprise to discover that one of her new coaches is none other than the great soccer legend Kulti. Although Sal had idolized Kulti her entire life, now she has nothing but</span>
  <span id="freeText12292476490552003384" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>"I have so much to teach you, Taco."</b>
</blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1546366652i/26845944._SX540_.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Kulti</b> is another masterfully crafted slow burn contemporary romance from the slow burn queen Mariana Zapata. Sal Casillas is a professional soccer player living in Houston, Texas. She has always been driven to achieve great things. When the new season is beginning, imagine her horror and surprise to discover that one of her new coaches is none other than the great soccer legend Kulti. Although Sal had idolized Kulti her entire life, now she has nothing but disdain in her heart for the cold soccer God. But when Sal recognizes the great man that Kulti is underneath all of the politics and flash and glam of the paparazzi, a friendship is formed. Kulti and Sal become best friends and their friendship soon develops into lasting love. With Kulti and Sal on the same team, there is nothing that can stop them! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466701540i/19510149._SX540_.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <b>"It doesn't matter. You'll go somewhere, and you aren't going alone."</b>
</blockquote> Told in multiple POV, <b>Kulti</b> is a passionate and tender-hearted read with complex characters, a well developed plot, and plenty of superstar soccer action. The dialogue is crafted with meticulous detail and every moment is thoroughly explored as the sexual tension builds the entire read. I adore the nuances in the character development of Kulti and Sal and how well they compliment each other perfectly. Truly there is always something magical when you open a Zapata book and with romance, complex characters, and a well-crafted plot <b>Kulti</b> is another must read! <blockquote>
  <b>"Hot wet lips grazed over my parted ones as he gripped my leg tightly. It was endless. His full mouth was the Pacific Ocean; it was huge and dark and wide and so, so easy to get lost in."</b>
</blockquote> Overall, I highly recommend <b>Kulti</b> to anyone who enjoys a slow burn romance with unforgettable characters and a masterfully crafted plot. Mariana Zapata is an expert storyteller and I look forward to reading more from this author!<br><br><b>* I am enjoying the audible version of this book! <br><br>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:<br><a href="https://craziesrusbookblog.wordpress.com//" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1483747845i/21645810.jpg" width="320" height="160" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450764696i/17467413.jpg" width="" height="30" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><a href="https://twitter.com/CraziesRus" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450633462i/17450183.png" width="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.pinterest.com/craziesrus/" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450763751i/17467332.jpg" width="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.facebook.com/Crazies-R-Us-Book-Blog-171506803016307/timeline/" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450633462i/17450182.png" width="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/110273454171852792166/posts" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451963666i/17626541.png" width="55" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450764696i/17467413.jpg" width="" height="30" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></b></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('4UjAJEuQg1WzwzxGLO3at8btw1dCn1rdZdu/HkhU6mpRU5nXTvwuxSdsPP8dop33CAhkh+Plg5Ke/KG/9fk36w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('v/iqJUXpZ0fshcEs/6eW/NIL7o9Q8x+sQGBIgSeATtgP4/PWQIXK13gqwZXO6NG8HO5JX/GJxuO7R1Ygmi2TWQ==')})
  }
